You can request funds by tapping on the BOARD on the Club Screen, but if you do, two things happen. Firstly, your BOARD relationship goes down and secondly, the BOARD will increase the shareholder cut of your post-match earnings. If your BOARD relationship is low, they will not release funds when requested.
